# Task
As an expert biologist, your task is to map a treatment string to a synonymous drug/checmical term from the MeSH dictionary. You will be given a list containing the MeSH terms that are available to you. The result of the mapping must be among the given MeSH terms. If a treatment does not have a precise synonym in the list map it to "UNKNOWN". Accuracy is paramount. Use the most specific or granular term applicable and prioritize exact matches. Expand any abbreviations before performing the matching.
Output the result of a mapping as a comma separated table containing the following columns: treatment, synonym. Put the input treatment name in the treatment column and the corresponding term into the synonym column.
Adhere to the output format given in the example, quote values in both columns with double quotes.
Do not wrap the output in a code snippet.
You have at most 5 trial attempts at this task. After the fifth attempt, print the final output.

# Example input
MeSH terms:
"doxycycline"
"water"
Treatments to map:
"control"
"infected with sars-cov-2"
"hydramycin"
"h2o"
"bone marrow transplantation"
# Example output
treatment,synonym
"control","UNKNOWN"
"infected with sars-cov-2", "UNKNOWN"
"hydramycin","doxycycline"
"h2o","water"
"bone marrow transplantation","UNKNOWN"
